//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);

reg [63:0] product;
reg [127:0] accumulator_reg;

always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator_reg <= 0;
    end else begin
        product <= A * B;
        accumulator_reg <= accumulator_reg + product;
    end
end

assign accumulator = accumulator_reg;

endmodule

//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.

    input wire clk,

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
    reg [63:0] product;
    reg [127:0] accumulator_reg;

    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            accumulator_reg <= 0;
        end else begin
            product <= A * B;
            accumulator_reg <= accumulator_reg + product;
        end
    end

    assign accumulator = accumulator_reg;

endmodule

//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
    
    reg [63:0] product;
    reg [127:0] accumulator_reg;
    
    always @(posedge clk) begin
        if (reset) begin
            accumulator_reg <= 0;
        end else begin
            product <= A * B;
            accumulator_reg <= accumulator_reg + product;
        end
    end
    
    assign accumulator = accumulator_reg;
    
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
  reg [63:0] product;
  reg [127:0] accumulator_reg;

  always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
      accumulator_reg <= 0;
    end else begin
      product <= A * B;
      accumulator_reg <= accumulator_reg + product;
    end
  end

  assign accumulator = accumulator_reg;

endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.

    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,

);

        accumulator <= 0;

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);

assign accumulator = (reset == 1'b1) ? 128'b0 : (accumulator + (A * B));

always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset == 1'b1) begin
        accumulator <= 128'b0;
    end
end

endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule

//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.

    input wire clk,

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @ (posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @ (posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);

parameter [127:0] zero = 0;

reg [63:0] product;
reg [127:0] accumulator_reg;

always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator_reg <= zero;
    end else begin
        product <= A * B;
        accumulator_reg <= accumulator_reg + product;
    end
end

assign accumulator = accumulator_reg;

endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if(reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);

integer i;
reg [63:0] product;
reg [127:0] accumulator_reg;

always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator_reg <= 0;
    end else begin
        product <= A * B;
        for (i = 0; i < 64; i = i + 1) begin
            accumulator_reg[i] <= accumulator_reg[i] ^ product[i];
        end
    end
end

assign accumulator = accumulator_reg;

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk, negedge reset) begin
    if (!reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if(reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk or negedge reset) begin
    if (reset == 0) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);


reg [63:0] product;
reg [127:0] accumulator_reg;

always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator_reg <= 0;
    end else begin
        product <= A * B;
        accumulator_reg <= accumulator_reg + product;
    end
end

assign accumulator = accumulator_reg;

endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if(reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if(reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
wire [127:0] product;
wire [127:0] accumulator_next;

assign product = A * B;

always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator_next;
    end
end

assign accumulator_next = accumulator + product;

endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset == 1) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);

    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);

  reg [63:0] product;
  reg [127:0] accumulator_reg;

  always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
      accumulator_reg <= 0;
    end else begin
      product <= A * B;
      accumulator_reg <= accumulator_reg + product;
    end
  end

  assign accumulator = accumulator_reg;

endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk, negedge reset) begin
    if (!reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk or negedge reset) begin
    if (reset == 0) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.

//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    accumulator <= {accumulator[126:0], A * B};
end

always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end
end

endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @ (posedge clk or posedge reset) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk)
begin
    if (reset)
        accumulator <= 0;
    else
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk or negedge reset) begin
    if (reset == 0) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);

wire [127:0] product;
wire [127:0] accumulated_product;

assign product = A * B;
assign accumulated_product = accumulator + product;

always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulated_product;
    end
end

endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);

reg signed [127:0] product;
reg signed [127:0] accumulator_reg;

always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator_reg <= 0;
    end else begin
        product <= A * B;
        accumulator_reg <= accumulator_reg + product;
    end
end

assign accumulator = accumulator_reg;

endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk, posedge reset) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 64'b0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk, posedge reset) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + (A * B);
    end
end
endmodule

//Design a Verilog module for a MAC (Multiplier and Accumulator) unit.
//The MAC unit takes two inputs, A and B, and multiplies them.
//The result of the multiplication is accumulated with a third register, C.
//The accumulated result is stored in an output register, accumulator.
//The module should have a control input, clk (clock), to synchronize the operations.
//The module should have a control input, reset (reset), to reset the accumulated result.
module mac_64(
    input wire clk,
    input wire reset,
    input wire [63:0] A,
    input wire [63:0] B,
    output reg [127:0] accumulator
);
always @(posedge clk) begin
    if (reset) begin
        accumulator <= 0;
    end else begin
        accumulator <= accumulator + A * B;
    end
end
endmodule
